#Amyz
# UI - nested custom loc
defined_text = {
	name = GetMinorityCultureUI
	text = { localisation_key =	AN_no_minority_culture_tooltip trigger = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 0 } } }
	text = { localisation_key = AN_minority_culture_tooltip	trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 } } }
}

defined_text = {
	name = GetSecondaryCultureUI
	text = { localisation_key =	AN_no_secondary_culture_tooltip trigger = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 0 } } }
	text = { localisation_key = AN_secondary_culture_tooltip	trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 1 } } }
}

defined_text = {
	name = GetMinorityReligionUI
	text = { localisation_key = AN_no_minority_religion_tooltip	trigger = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_religion_size value = 0 } } }
	text = { localisation_key = AN_minority_religion_tooltip	trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion_size value = 1 } } }
}

defined_text = {
	name = GetSecondaryReligionUI
	text = { localisation_key = AN_no_secondary_religion_tooltip	trigger = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_secondary_religion value = 0 } } }
	text = { localisation_key = AN_secondary_religion_tooltip	trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_secondary_religion value = 1 } } }
}

###

defined_text = {
	name = GetMajorityCultureSize
	text = { localisation_key = AN_totality_culture_tooltip trigger = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 0 } } }
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_supermajority_culture_tooltip 
		trigger = { 
			is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 }
			is_variable_equal = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 0 } 
		} 
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_majority_culture_tooltip 
		trigger = { 
			OR = { 
				AND = { 
					is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 2 } 
					is_variable_equal = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 0 } 
				} 
				AND = { 
					is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 } 
					check_variable = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 1 } 
				} 
			} 
		} 
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_slim_majority_culture_tooltip 
		trigger = { 
			OR = { 
				AND = { 
					is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 3 } 
					is_variable_equal = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 0 } 
				} 
				AND = { 
					is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 2 } 
					check_variable = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 1 } 
				} 
			} 
		} 
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_plurality_culture_tooltip 
		trigger = { 
			is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 3 } 
			check_variable = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 1 } 
		} 
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = GetMajorityReligionSize
	text = { localisation_key = AN_totality_religion_tooltip trigger = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_religion_size value = 0 } } }
	text = { localisation_key = AN_supermajority_religion_tooltip trigger = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_religion_size value = 1 } is_variable_equal = { which = AN_secondary_religion value = 0 } } }
	text = { localisation_key = AN_majority_religion_tooltip trigger = { OR = { AND = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_religion_size value = 2 } is_variable_equal = { which = AN_secondary_religion value = 0 } } AND = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_religion_size value = 1 } check_variable = { which = AN_secondary_religion value = 1 } } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = AN_slim_majority_religion_tooltip trigger = { OR = { AND = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_religion_size value = 3 } is_variable_equal = { which = AN_secondary_religion value = 0 } } AND = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_religion_size value = 2 } check_variable = { which = AN_secondary_religion value = 1 } } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = AN_plurality_religion_tooltip trigger = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_religion_size value = 3 } check_variable = { which = AN_secondary_religion value = 1 } } }
}

defined_text = {
	name = GetMinorityCultureSize
	text = { localisation_key = AN_small_culture_minority trigger = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 } } } 
	text = { localisation_key = AN_significant_culture_minority trigger = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 2 } } } 
	text = { localisation_key = AN_large_culture_minority trigger = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 3 } } }
}

defined_text = {
	name = GetMajorityCultureType
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_primary_culture
		trigger = {
			owner = { primary_culture = variable:PREV:AN_province_culture }
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_unified_culture
		trigger = {
			owner = { accepted_culture = variable:PREV:AN_province_culture culture_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_culture }
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_accepted_culture
		trigger = {
			owner = { accepted_culture = variable:PREV:AN_province_culture }
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_coexisting_culture
		trigger = {
			owner = { culture_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_culture }
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_protected_culture
		trigger = {
			owner = { NOT = { culture_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_culture } }
			has_province_flag = AN_protect_maj
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_nonaccepted_culture
		trigger = {
			owner = { NOT = { culture_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_culture } }
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_enslaved_culture
		trigger = {
			owner = { NOT = { culture_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_culture } }
			has_province_flag = AN_enslave_maj
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_expelled_culture
		trigger = {
			owner = { NOT = { culture_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_culture } }
			has_province_flag = AN_expel_maj
		}
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = GetMajorityReligionType
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_truefaith_religion
		trigger = {
			owner = { religion = variable:PREV:AN_province_religion }
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_syncretic_religion
		trigger = {
			owner = { secondary_religion = variable:PREV:AN_province_religion }
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_tol_htc_religion
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					owner = { religion_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_religion }
					owner = { check_variable = { which = AN_tol_htc value = 0 } }
				}
				AND = {
					owner = { religion_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_religion }
					owner = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_tol_htc value = 0 } } }
					has_province_flag = AN_tolerate_maj	
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_int_htc_religion
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					owner = { religion_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_religion }
					owner = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_tol_htc value = 0 } } }
				}
				AND = {
					owner = { religion_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_religion }
					owner = { check_variable = { which = AN_tol_htc value = 0 } }
					has_province_flag = AN_persecute_maj	
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_tol_hth_religion
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					owner = { NOT = { religion_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_religion } }
					owner = { check_variable = { which = AN_tol_hth value = 0 } }
				}
				AND = {
					owner = { NOT = { religion_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_religion } }
					owner = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_tol_hth value = 0 } } }
					has_province_flag = AN_tolerate_maj	
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = AN_int_hth_religion
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					owner = { NOT = { religion_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_religion } }
					owner = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_tol_hth value = 0 } } }
				}
				AND = {
					owner = { NOT = { religion_group = variable:PREV:AN_province_religion } }
					owner = { check_variable = { which = AN_tol_hth value = 0 } }
					has_province_flag = AN_persecute_maj	
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#RELIGION GROUP
defined_text = {
	name = GetMinorityReligionGroup

	text = { localisation_key = christian trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 1 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 13 } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = muslim trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 13 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 18 } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = eastern trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 18 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 24 } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = dharmic trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 24 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 28 } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = pagan trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 28 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 35 } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = caucus_pagan trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 35 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 39 } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = asian_pagan trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 39 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 46 } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = african_pagan trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 46 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 53 } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = oceanic_pagan trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 53 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 55 } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = american_pagan trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 55 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 59 } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = tribal_beliefs trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 59 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 60 } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = jewish_group trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 60 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 61 } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = zoroastrian_group trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 61 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 65 } } } }
	text = { localisation_key = chthonic_religion_group trigger = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 65 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_religion value = 66 } } } }

}

defined_text = {
	name = GetSecondaryReligionGroup
